<Z>PDF Problems <C> A few players over the last few weeks have had some problems with their anti-virus deciding to prevent them <L.31.1>
accessing a game report, possibly suggesting there is a virus (there isn't) or not suggesting anything. We haven't changed anything,<L.31.1>
so I'm afraid there's little we can do (I have a pretty grim workaround if necessary) so if you do get the problem, I suggest have <L.31.1>
a look at the Latest News on the website, where I will post whatever I can, but really you need to bug your provider to fix their <L.31.1>
algorithm. It's far from ideal I know, very frustrating from your perspective (and mine)...<L.31.1>

the system will only take the latest set, but if they're spread out both may be input and you'll get charged 0.1 credit.<L.31.1>
